    SELECT TOP(1) [a].[Id], [a].[AppointmentDate], [a].[CreatedAt], [a].[DoctorId], [a].[Notes], [a].[PatientId], [a].[Status], [p].[Id] AS [Id0], [p].[Address], [p].[BloodGroup], [p].[DateOfBirth], [p].[Gender], [p].[Phone], [p].[UserId], [u].[Id] AS [Id1], [u].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [u].[Email], [u].[FullName], [u].[PasswordHash], [u].[Role], [d].[Id] AS [Id2], [d].[ConsultationFee], [d].[IsAvailable], [d].[LicenseNumber], [d].[Phone] AS [Phone0], [d].[UserId] AS [UserId0], [d].[YearsOfExperience], [u0].[Id] AS [Id3], [u0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt1], [u0].[Email] AS [Email0], [u0].[FullName] AS [FullName0], [u0].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash0], [u0].[Role] AS [Role0], [p0].[Id] AS [Id4], [p0].[AppointmentId], [p0].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt2], [p0].[Diagnosis], [p0].[Notes] AS [Notes0]
    FROM [Appointments] AS [a]
    INNER JOIN [Patients] AS [p] ON [a].[PatientId] = [p].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [p].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Doctors] AS [d] ON [a].[DoctorId] = [d].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u0] ON [d].[UserId] = [u0].[Id]
    LEFT JOIN [Prescriptions] AS [p0] ON [a].[Id] = [p0].[AppointmentId]
    WHERE [a].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [Medicines] AS [m] ON [t].[Id4] = [m].[PrescriptionId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t].[Id2], [t].[Id3], [t].[Id4]
